select dccocodi dccocodi, 
dccotdco||' - '||tdcodesc dccotdco, 
dccofefa||' - '||fefadesc dccofefa, 
cc_boBssCollectData.fsbAddress(dccoiddi) dccoiddi, 
dccodeco dccodeco, 
dccodebc||' - '||cc_boBssDescription.fsbState(dccodebc) dccodebc, 
dccolobc||' - '||cc_boBssDescription.fsbCity(dccodebc, dccolobc) dccolobc, 
dccobadc||' - '||barrdesc dccobadc, 
dccodezp||' - '||cc_boBssDescription.fsbState(dccodezp) dccodezp, 
dccolozp||' - '||cc_boBssDescription.fsbCity(dccodezp, dccolozp) dccolozp, 
dccozopo||' - '||zopodesc dccozopo, 
dccotcba||' - '||tcbadesc dccotcba, 
dccobanc||' - '||bancnomb dccobanc, 
dccosuba||' - '||subanomb dccosuba, 
dccocuco dccoccuco, 
dccovetc dccovetc, 
dccodade||' - '||cc_boBssDescription.fsbState(dccodade) dccodade, 
dccodalo||' - '||cc_boBssDescription.fsbCity(dccodade, dccodalo) dccodalo, 
cc_boBssCollectData.fsbAddress(dccoidda) dccoidda, 
:parent_id parent_id
from dicocobr, suscripc, tidicobr, foenfact, barrio, zonapost, ticubanc, banco, sucubanc
where 
suscdcco = dccocodi AND
dccotdco = tdcocodi AND
dccofefa = fefacodi AND
dccodebc = barrdepa AND dccolobc = barrloca AND dccobadc = barrcodi AND
dccodezp = zopodepa AND dccolozp = zopoloca AND dccozopo = zopocodi AND
dccotcba = tcbacodi AND
dccobanc = banccodi AND
dccobanc = subabanc AND dccosuba = subacodi
 AND susccodi = :inuContract
